<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глушить.html>глуши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оглядка.html>огля́дка</a> (14605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оглядеть.html>огляде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogljadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оглядка.html>огля́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogljádka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оглядка.html>огля́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оглядка.html>огля́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оглядка.html>огля́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> looking back
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оглядка.html>огля́дки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bežátʹ bez ogljádki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">run as fast as one can</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> care, caution
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:действовать.html>де́йствовать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оглядка.html>огля́дкой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">déjstvovatʹ s ogljádkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">act circumspectly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:оглядка.html>огля́дкой</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-л</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>ogljádkoj</b> na kovó-l</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">while watching the reaction of smb</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оглядывавшийся.html>огля́дывавшийся</a> (2215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оглядывавшийся.html>огля́дывавшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogljádyvavšijsja</span>)
</p>

***огневой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:огневой.html>огнево́й</a> (5425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogónʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogónʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> comes ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁n̥gʷnis</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">igneous</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">containing, resembling or produced by fire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огневой.html>огнево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ognevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:огневой.html>огнева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мощь.html>мощь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ognevája</b> moščʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fire</b>power</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:огневой.html>огнева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завеса.html>заве́са</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ognevája</b> zavésa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">curtain of fire</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>fire</b> curtain</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:огневой.html>огнева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ognevája</b> tóčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">weapon emplacement</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>fire</b> point</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:огневой.html>огнево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубеж.html>рубе́ж</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ognevój</b> rubéž</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>firing</b> line</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fiery, passionate</li>
<li>fervent, ardent, boisterous, perky, full of life/pep</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огненный.html>о́гненный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ógnennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:огненный.html>о́гненный</a> (3536)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огненный.html>о́гненный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ógnennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:огненный.html>о́гненный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:маршал.html>ма́ршал</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ógnennyj</b> máršal</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>fire</b> marshal</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fiery
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гее́нна <b><a href = vnd.unilang:огненный.html>о́гненная</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gejénna <b>ógnennaja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Gehenna, blazing inferno, raging inferno, roaring inferno</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>fiery</b> Gehenna</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogónʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тушить.html>туши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Feuerlöscher</i>.

***ого.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ого.html>ого́</a> (5863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ого.html>ого́</a>!</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ohó</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogó</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>whoa; oh, ho!; wow!; oh, my goodness!; oh, oh! (expresses surprise, admiration, approval, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ого.html>ого́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырасти.html>вы́рос</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ogó</b>, kak ty výros!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Wow, how you’ve grown!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ого.html>ого́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Naródu tam — <b>ogó</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The people there—oh, oh, oh!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ого.html>ого́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гриб.html>грибо́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́л</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ogó</b>, skólʹko gribóv ty sobrál!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Wow, so many mushrooms you collected!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорить.html>оговори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogovorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговаривать.html>огова́ривать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogovárivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***оговорить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оговорить.html>оговори́ть</a> (16303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорить.html>оговори́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogovorítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговаривать.html>огова́ривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander</li>
<li>to stipulate</li>
<li>to mention, to specify</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оговориться.html>оговори́ться</a> (16661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорить.html>оговори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogovorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговориться.html>оговори́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogovorítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговариваться.html>огова́риваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make a slip of the tongue</li>
<li>to make a reservation or stipulation
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1964</b>,  Юрий Осипович Домбровский (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yury_Dombrovsky" class="extiw" title="w:Yury Dombrovsky">Yury Osipovich Dombrovsky</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:хранитель.html>Храни́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:древность.html>дре́вностей</a></cite>, part 1, chapter 2 |  translated as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Glenny" class="extiw" title="w:Michael Glenny">Michael Glenny</a>, transl., <cite>The Keeper of Antiquities</cite>, Carcanet, 1969, page 30:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>Здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:оговориться.html>оговори́ться</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>пишу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:абстрактный.html>абстра́ктном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сстве</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:абстракция.html>абстра́кции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сстве</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совсем.html>совсе́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разный.html>ра́зные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>ве́щи</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zdesʹ núžno <b>ogovorítʹsja</b>. Ja pišú ne ob abstráktnom iskússtve, a ob abstrákcii v iskússtve, a éto sovsém ráznyje véšči.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Here I must <b>make myself clear</b>. I am not discussing abstract but abstraction in art; they are two completely different things.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорить.html>оговори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogovorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***оговорка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оговорка.html>огово́рка</a> (13255)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорить.html>оговори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogovorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорка.html>огово́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogovórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорка.html>огово́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорка.html>огово́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорка.html>огово́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reservation, proviso, stipulation, ifs
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оговорка.html>огово́ркой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s ogovórkoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with reserve</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оговорка.html>огово́рок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez ogovórok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">without reserve; unreservedly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>slip of the tongue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оговорка.html>огово́рка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> фре́йду</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ogovórka po frɛ́jdu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Freudian slip</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ifs, ands, or buts</li>
<li>caveat, clause, reservation, disclaimer</li></ol>

***оголить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оголить.html>оголи́ть</a> (13421)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голый.html>го́лый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gólyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оголить.html>оголи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogolítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оголя́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bare, to strip</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оголить.html>оголи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фланг.html>фланг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ogolítʹ</b> flang</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to expose the flank</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***оголтелый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оголтелый.html>оголте́лый</a> (21738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оголтелый.html>оголте́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogoltélyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unbridled, rampant, frenzied, wild, extreme
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оголтелый.html>оголте́лый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:национализм.html>национали́зм</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ogoltélyj</b> nacionalízm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">unbridled nationalism</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оголте́л, оголте́ла, оголте́ло, оголте́лы</span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their appearing similar to past-tense forms.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="2" bgcolor="EEF9FF" rowspan="2" style="vertical-align:center;"><a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a></th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF" colspan="3" align="center"> ед. ч.</th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF" rowspan="2" align="center" style="vertical-align:center;"> мн. ч.</th>
</tr><tr bgcolor="EEF9FF">
<th> муж. р. </th><th> ср. р. </th><th> жен. р. </th>
</tr><tr>

***огонь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a> (436)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">огнь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ognĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ogňь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*ugnis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁n̥gʷnis</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ignition</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">igneous</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">uguns</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ignis</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">अग्नि</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">agní</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hittite_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hittite language">Hittite</a></span> <i class="Xsux mention" lang="hit">𒀀𒀝𒉌𒅖</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hit-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">a-ak-ni-iš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an Indo-Aryan borrowing.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogónʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огня́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огни́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>огне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fire <i>(also figurative)</i></li>
<li>light</li>
<li>weapons fire</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:огородить.html>огороди́ть</a> (11601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:городить.html>городи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to surround with a fence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огородить.html>огороди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogorodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">огора́живать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fence in, to enclose</li></ol>

***огорошить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:огорошить.html>огоро́шить</a> (31528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, perhaps a modification of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огородить.html>огороди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ogorodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fence in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лапо́шить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lapóšitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:копошиться.html>копоши́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kopošítʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to swarm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:огорошить.html>огоро́шить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ogoróšitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take aback, to disconcert
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:огорошить.html>огоро́шило</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó éto <b>ogoróšilo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was <b>disconcerted [taken aback]</b> by that</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
